(function InlineTTIMarker() {
  function windowPerformance() {
    var perf =
      window.performance ||
      window.mozPerformance ||
      window.msPerformance ||
      window.webkitPerformance ||
      {};
    var perfNow = perf.now || perf.mozNow || perf.msNow || perf.webkitNow;
    if (perfNow) {
      if (!perf.mark) {
        perf.mark = function () {};
      }
      if (!perf.measure) {
        perf.measure = function () {};
      }
      if (!perf.now) {
        perf.now = perfNow;
      }
      return perf;
    }
    return {
      now: function () {
        return Date.now();
      },
      mark: function () {},
      measure: function () {},
    };
  }
  function performanceNowFromEpoch() {
    if (window.performance && window.performance.now) {
      return (
        window.performance.timing.navigationStart + window.performance.now()
      );
    }
    return Date.now();
  }
  var performance = windowPerformance();
  var requestStart = performance.timing.requestStart
    ? performance.timing.requestStart
    : Date.now();
  window.__markInlineTTI = function () {
    window.__INLINE_TTI = performanceNowFromEpoch() - requestStart;
    performance.measure("Time to AirbnbInteractive");
  };
  window.__getMarkedInlineTTI = function () {
    return window.__INLINE_TTI;
  };
  window.__clearMarkedInlineTTI = function () {
    window.__INLINE_TTI = undefined;
  };
  window.__markInlineTTI();
